* $Header: M:/default/input/RCS/dict.txt,v 1.560 2021/05/18 14:10:31 avk Exp $
* "FILER" DICTIONARY FILE.  CONTAINS LAYOUT OF COMMON BLOCKS USED FOR THE FILER PROGRAM.
* RECORDS IN THIS FILE STARTING WITH A NON-BLANK CHARACTER ARE COMMENTS.
* THIS DICTIONARY FILE IS FORMATTED AS FOLLOWS:
* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*
* ARRAY DIMENSION RECORDS:
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
* COLUMNS  VARIABLE     DESCRIPTION
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
*   2--4   DIM          KEYWORD USED BY FILER
*   7-12   FDimNam      DIMENSION MNEMONIC
*  16-18   FDimSiz      DIMENSION SIZE
*  25-49   FDimDescrip  DIMENSION DESCRIPTION
*
* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*
* COMMON BLOCK ATTRIBUTE RECORDS:
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
* COLUMNS  VARIABLE     DESCRIPTION
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
*   2--4   ATT          KEYWORD USED BY FILER
*   6--6   L            "L" INDICATES AN ATTRIBUTE LABEL; " " (A BLANK) INDICATES AN ATTRIBUTE VALUE
*   8-13   FAttNam      ATTRIBUTE NAME
*  16-40   FAttDescrip  ATTRIBUTE DESCRIPTION
*
* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*
* GLOBAL DATA STRUCTURE RECORDS:
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
* COLUMNS  VARIABLE     DESCRIPTION
* -------  --------     ------------------------------------------------------
*   2-17   FBLKNM(I)    COMMON BLOCK NAME. NEED NOT REPEAT.  (16 CHARS)
*  19-34   FVARNM(I)    VARIABLE NAME (16 CHARS)
*  36-36   FVARTY(I)    VARIABLE TYPE: R=REAL, I=INTEGER, C=CHARACTER (1 CHAR)
*  38-41   FVARLN(I)    VARIABLE LENGTH (R: 4 OR 8; I: 2 OR 4; C:1 TO 9999)
*  43-43   FNDIMS(I)    NUMBER OF DIMENSIONS  (1 CHAR)
*  46-79   FKDIM(5,I)   SIZE OF EACH DIMENSION (5 FIELDS OF 6 CHARS EACH WITH A SPACE IN BETWEEN)
*  81-114  FATTR(5,I)   ATTRIBUTE TYPE (5 FIELDS OF 6 CHARS EACH)
* 116-165  FDESCR(I)    DESCRIPTION (48 CHARS)
*
* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*****************************************************************************************************************************************************************

*  The following line (containing equal signs), and all similar lines scattered through this dictionary, ends at the point filer stops reading the description.
*  Typing beyond there is fine, as it comments the variable here, but filer is not picking it up to use elsewhere.
*================ ================ = ==== =  ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ========================================
*FBLKNM           FVARNM           FVARTY FNDIMS    ?      ?      ?      ?       ?      ?      ?      ?      ?
*?                ?                ? FVARLN  ?      ?      ?      ?      ?       ?      ?      ?      ?      FDESCR
*?                ?                ? ?    ?  (FKDIM(K), K= 1, 5)  ?      ?      (FATTR(K), K= 1,4)   ?      ?
*================ ================ = ==== =  ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ====== ==================================================
* Quantities Common Block
